DUS NGAN TSEN GANG ZHIG DAM CHOS PHYAG RGYA

'DI 'DZIN PA, ,DE YI BZOD DANG BRTZON 'GRUS 'DI NI MTSUNGS MED
SHES RAB GZHAL DU MED, ,DE NAS DE BZHIN GSHEGS PA TING NGE 'DZIN
RDUL DANG BRAL BA'I STOBS KYIS RNAM PAR GNON

PAS KYANG 'DI SKAD CES BKA' STZAL TO, ,GANG GIS MDO 'DI BSHAD NAS
BZUNG DANG MNGON PAR BRIS PA DANG, ,GZHAN DAG 'DZIN BCUG GUS PAR
RTAG TU KLOG PA DANG, ,BDUG PA ME

TOG PHRENG BA GOS MCHOG RNAMS KYIS MCHOD, ,BSOD NAMS GANG THOB DE
NI BRJOD PAR MI NUS SO, ,DE NAS SANGS RGYAS BCOM LDAN 'DAS TSAD
MED GRANGS MED PA DE DAG GIS MDO SDE


@432A *, ,'DI'I BSNGAGS PA DANG, YON TAN DANG, PHAN YON DPAG TU
MED PAR BRJOD NAS BRGYA BYIN DANG, TSANGS PA DANG, 'JIG RTEN
SKYONG BA DE DAG LA BOS TE 'DI

SKAD CES BKA' STZAL TO, ,KYE GROGS PO DAG, LAS KYI SGRIB PA DANG,
NYON MONGS PA THAMS CAD BYANG BAR BYED PA, PHYI MA'I DUS NA GANG
THOS PA TZAM GYIS KYANG SEMS CAN RNAMS KYI

LAS KYI SGRIB PA DANG, NYON MONGS PA THAMS CAD ZAD PAR 'GYUR BA'I
CHOS KYI RNAM GRANGS 'DI ZUNGS SHIG, BCOM LDAN 'DAS KYIS DE SKAD
CES BKA' STZAL NAS THAMS CAD

DANG LDAN PA'I 'KHOR DANG, LHA DANG, MI DANG, LHA MA YIN DANG,
DRI ZAR BCAS PA'I 'JIG RTEN YI RANG STE BCOM LDAN 'DAS KYIS
GSUNGS PA LA MNGON PAR BSTOD DO, ,'DUS PA

CHEN PO RIN PO CHE TOG GI GZUNGS LAS, MTHAR PHYIN PA'I LE'U STE
BCU GSUM PA'O,, ,,'PHAGS PA 'DUS PA CHEN PO RIN PO CHE TOG GI
GZUNGS ZHES BYA BA THEG PA CHEN

PO'I MDO RDZOGS SO,, ,,RGYA GAR GYI MKHAN PO SH'I LENDRA BO DHI
DANG, ZHU CHEN GYI LO TZ'A BA BANDHE YE SHES SDES ZHUS TE SKAD
GSAR BCAD KYIS KYANG BCOS NAS GTAN LA PHAB PA,
